<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-batchaggregator"></a>

### `BatchAggregator`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/BatchAggregator.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait BatchAggregator[A, B] extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

This batch aggregator exposes a BatchAggregator.run method that allows for batching scala.concurrent.Future computations, defined by a BatchAggregator.Processor.

**Signature**

```text
object ByteStringUtil
```

**Summary**

If maxBytesToRead is not specified, we decompress all the gunzipper input stream. If maxBytesToRead is specified, we decompress maximum maxBytesToRead bytes, and if the input is larger we throw MaxBytesToDecompressExceeded error.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-chainutil"></a>

### `ChainUtil`

- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/ChainUtil$.html)

**Signature**

```text
object ChainUtil
```

**Summary**

Provides utility functions for the cats implementation of a Chain. This is a data-structure similar to a List, with constant time prepend and append. Note that the Chain has a performance hit when pattern matching as there is no constant-time uncons operation.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-checked"></a>

### `Checked`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/Checked.html)

**Signature**

```text
sealed abstract class Checked[+A, +N, +R] extends Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

A monad for aborting and non-aborting errors. Non-aborting errors are accumulated in a cats.data.Chain until the first aborting error is hit. You can think of com.digitalasset.canton.util.Checked as an extension of Either to also support errors that should not cause the computation to abort.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-checkedt"></a>

### `CheckedT`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/CheckedT.html)

**Signature**

```text
final case class CheckedT[F[_], A, N, R](value: F[Checked[A, N, R]]) extends Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

Monad Transformer for Checked, allowing the effect of a monad F to be combined with the aborting and non-aborting failure effect of Checked. Similar to cats.data.EitherT.

**Signature**

```text
final class LazyValWithContext[T, Context] extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

"Implements" a lazy val field whose initialization expression can refer to implicit context information of type Context. The "val" is initialized upon the first call to get, using the context information supplied for this call, like a lazy val.

- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/LengthLimitedByteString.html)

**Signature**

```text
sealed trait LengthLimitedByteString extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

This trait wraps a ByteString that is limited to a certain maximum length. Classes implementing this trait expose create and tryCreate methods to safely (and non-safely) construct such a ByteString.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-orderedbucketmergehub"></a>

### `OrderedBucketMergeHub`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/OrderedBucketMergeHub.html)

**Signature**

```text
class OrderedBucketMergeHub[Name, A, Config, Offset, M] extends GraphStageWithMaterializedValue[FlowShape[OrderedBucketMergeConfig[Name, Config], Output[Name, (Config, Option[M]), A, Offset]], Future[Done]] with NamedLogging
```

**Summary**

A custom Pekko org.apache.pekko.stream.stage.GraphStage that merges several ordered source streams into one based on those sources reaching a threshold for equivalent elements.

**Members**

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-pekkoutil"></a>

### `PekkoUtil`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/PekkoUtil$.html)

**Signature**

```text
object PekkoUtil extends HasLoggerName
```

**Summary**

Delegates to a future org.apache.pekko.stream.KillSwitch once the kill switch becomes available. If both com.digitalasset.canton.util.PekkoUtil.DelayedKillSwitch.shutdown and com.digitalasset.canton.util.PekkoUtil.DelayedKillSwitch.abort are called or com.digitalasset.canton.util.PekkoUtil.DelayedKillSwitch.abort is called multiple times before the delegate is available, then the winning call is non-deterministic.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-reassignmenttag"></a>

### `ReassignmentTag`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/ReassignmentTag.html)

**Signature**

```text
sealed trait ReassignmentTag[+T] extends Product with Serializable
```

**Summary**

In reassignment transactions, we deal with two synchronizers: the source synchronizer and the target synchronizer. The Source and Target wrappers help differentiate between these two synchronizers, allowing us to manage their specific characteristics, such as protocol versions, static synchronizer parameters, and other synchronizer-specific details.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-samereassignmenttype"></a>

### `SameReassignmentType`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/SameReassignmentType.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait SameReassignmentType[T[_]] extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

A type class that ensures the reassignment type remains consistent across multiple parameters of a method. This is useful when dealing with types that represent different reassignment contexts (e.g., Source and Target), and we want to enforce that all parameters share the same reassignment context.

**Members**

No members found for this type in the configured artifacts.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-setcover"></a>

### `SetCover`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/SetCover$.html)

**Signature**

```text
object SetCover
```

**Summary**

Let universe be the union of all elements in all the sets in sets. Selects a subset of sets so that their union equals universe, i.e. a cover as specified by covered. The returned cover is in general neither minimal nor unique.

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

**Signature**

```text
class SimpleExecutionQueue extends PrettyPrinting with NamedLogging with FlagCloseableAsync with ExecutionQueue
```

**Summary**

Functions executed with this class will only run when all previous calls have completed executing. This can be used when async code should not be run concurrently.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-singleusecell"></a>

### `SingleUseCell`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/SingleUseCell.html)

**Signature**

```text
class SingleUseCell[A] extends AnyRef
```

**Summary**

This class provides a mutable container for a single value of type A. The value may be put at most once. A SingleUseCell therefore provides the following immutability guarantee: The value of a cell cannot change; once it has been put there, it will remain in the cell.

<a id="type-com-digitalasset-canton-util-thereafterasync"></a>

### `ThereafterAsync`

- Introduced: `3.4.10`
- Deprecated: -
- Removed: -

Upstream docs: [Open](https://docs.digitalasset.com/operate/3.4/scaladoc/com/digitalasset/canton/util/ThereafterAsync.html)

**Signature**

```text
trait ThereafterAsync[F[_]] extends Thereafter[F]
```

**Summary**

Extension of Thereafter that adds the possibility to run an asynchronous piece of code afterwards with proper synchronization and exception propagation.
